build-not-bin-vergil:
     [echo] 
     [echo] 	$PTII/bin/vergil does not exist, perhaps (cd $PTII/bin; make) has not been run?
     [echo] 	This can happen if the make binary cannot be found in the path or if $PTII/mk/ptII.mk
     [echo] 	is not present.
     [echo] 	Skipping running make in $PTII/bin, which creates scripts like $PTII/bin/vergil.
     [echo] 	This is only an issue if you want to invoke "$PTII/bin/vergil" instead of "ant vergil".
     [echo] 	However, $PTII/bin does include other scripts that may be of use.
     [echo]

     [echo]      The default is to run all the fairly short-running tests.
     [echo]      On a fast machine, these tests take around 30 minutes.
     [echo] 
     [echo]      To run different tests, use -Dtest.batch, for example:
     [echo]         ant test.short -Dtest.batch=ptolemy/domains/continuous/**/junit/*.java
     [echo] 
     [echo]       test - builds and runs test.short, test.long and test.longest
     [echo]       test.32bit - runs the 32-bit JVM tests in auto32/
     [echo]       test.long - runs tests that are fairly long (called by the test target)
     [echo]       test.longest - runs tests that are longest (called by the test target)
     [echo]       test.report.all - runs batch of tests specified by a path with wildcards (output=files)
     [echo]       test.report.short - runs tests that are fairly fast, generates JUnit xml
     [echo]       test.short - runs tests that are fairly fast (~30 min., called by the test target)
